<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">milliard</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral_2">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***миловать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:миловать.html>милова́ть</a> (19836)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:миловать.html>ми́ловать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mílovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помиловать.html>поми́ловать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to show mercy <i>(to)</i>, to pardon, to grant pardon <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:миловать.html>миловал</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">box miloval</i> ― <span class="e-translation">God has been merciful (to somebody); the Lord has spared (somebody)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:миловать.html>милова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">milovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to caress, to fondle</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:милый.html>ми́лый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mílyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдце</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sérdce</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, literally "kindheartedness".

***милостивый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:милостивый.html>ми́лостивый</a> (8267)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:милость.html>ми́лость</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mílostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:милостивый.html>ми́лостивый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mílostivyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> merciful, gracious, kind
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:милостивый.html>ми́лостивый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:государь.html>госуда́рь</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обращение.html>обраще́нии</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mílostivyj</b> gosudárʹ (v obraščénii)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sir; <i>(in a letter)</i> Sir; <i>(less officially)</i> Dear Sir</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:милостивый.html>ми́лостивая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:государыня.html>госуда́рыня</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обращение.html>обраще́нии</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mílostivaja</b> gosudárynja (v obraščénii)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">madam; <i>(in a letter)</i> Madam; <i>(less officially)</i> Dear Madam</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:милость.html>ми́лость</a> (4109)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*milostь</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:милость.html>ми́лость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mílostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:милость.html>ми́лости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:милость.html>ми́лости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:милость.html>ми́лостей</a></b>)

***милый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:милый.html>ми́лый</a> (17300)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">милъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">milŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*milъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:милый.html>ми́лый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mílyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)миле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:миля.html>миле́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dear, sweet (having a pleasing disposition)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насильно.html>наси́льно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:милый.html>мил</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дешь</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nasílʹno mil ne búdešʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">love cannot be compelled</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:милый.html>ми́лый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mílyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:милый.html>ми́лого</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:милый.html>ми́лые</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:милый.html>ми́лых</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:милый.html>ми́лая</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>beloved</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in direct address<span class="ib-comma">,</span> also ironic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dear, darling</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мимоходом.html>мимохо́дом</a> (11369)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мимо.html>ми́мо</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mímo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ход</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-xod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ом</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-om</span>, <span class="ann-pos">instrumental suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, based on a combining form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to walk, to go</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***мина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мина.html>ми́на</a> (2590)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Mine</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мина.html>ми́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мина.html>ми́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мина.html>ми́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мина.html>ми́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mine (exploding device)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mortar round</li>
<li>grimace, face</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> torpedo</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mine (underground tunnel packed with explosives)</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">minaret</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish language">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota">مناره</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ota-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">minare</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">مناره</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">menâre</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">مَنَارَة</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">manāra</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lighthouse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***минеральный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:минеральный.html>минера́льный</a> (8002)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:минерал.html>минера́л</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">minerál</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:минеральный.html>минера́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">minerálʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)минера́льнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)минера́льней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mineral
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:минеральный.html>минера́льная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>вода́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>minerálʹnaja</b> vodá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">mineral water</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:минеральный.html>минера́льное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:питание.html>пита́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>minerálʹnoje</b> pitánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">mineral nutrition, inorganic nutrition</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>full of minerals <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">especially of wine</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***минировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:минировать.html>мини́ровать</a> (26385)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мина.html>ми́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:минировать.html>мини́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">minírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:минировать.html>мини́ровать</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заминировать.html>замини́ровать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mine <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to lay mines in</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
